 '- input IANS With the arrival of Makar Sankranti, the weather has taken a turn in entire North India including delhi-ncr

 Generally, due to Makar Sankranti, the cold starts decreasing, but this time it is going to reverse

 This was confirmed by the rain that occurred on Wednesday morning

 According to the information given officially, on the fifth festival bath, a confluence of reverence, devotion and tradition will be seen on the banks of Kshipra, especially Ram Ghat, Dutt Akhara and Triveni Ghat
 snaan parv main bhaag lene ke liye shraddhaluon kaa mahakaal kii nagari ujjayini pahunchnaa mangalvaar se hi shuru ho gaya he
